I had high hopes for this restaurant since it is so close to our house.   Today was the third time for me to try A Taste Above and the third time I was disappointed.  The first time I tried the bulgogi fries and they had hardly any meat and didn‚Äôt taste fresh.  I was left feeling unsatisfied and hungry after eating.  The second time I ordered banh mi and again it had hardly any meat and bun was not fresh.  I also waited for 30 minutes. Today I went in to order and after ordering the cashier told me it was going to be 45 minutes before the food was ready.  I ended up asking for my money back.  I think the banner hanging on the side of building where an actual sign belongs is a good indication of the mismanaged operation.  The restaurant is always cluttered and a mess on the inside.  It seems as if the owners put saving money before providing good food and customer service.  With no one else in the restaurant I‚Äôm not sure how it would take 45 minutes to cook 1 hamburger.  I would recommend skipping this place.</Review>

<rate>5< /rate>< Review>
I am the worst about giving review on places, things I order online, etc., but this spin gym is well worth the effort. I have done spin at a number of spin studios throughout Newport  Beach and Costa Mesa over the past 3 years, and have committed to Freedom Ride in Newport Beach for the past 6 months. I have watched my stamina and strength increase, all the while watching my body change. I go a minimum of 3 times a week, usually 4-5 times, on top of other work outs I have incorporated in addition to spin. I am down 20 pounds, just in time for my wedding, and I have the wonderful people at Freedom Ride to thank! It is exactly the friendly fun and motivation I needed to get back into an active life style. I now can't imagine my life without it! Chris, the owner, has always been very accommodating with any questions or concerns I might have, and my two favorite trainers are Taryn and Erica. Both are extremely welcoming, have AWESOME music.They really know how to "get down"! If you're in for making new friends, learning some new dance moves, and are willing to "work your face off", literally, girls walk out without eyebrows after, this is for you!! Thanks Freedom for helping me get my health back! Love ya!</Review>

< text>
Freedom is very clean, friendly, welcoming and aesthetically pleasing studio. The interior design is open and chic, and you can tell a lot of hard work was put it to make this studio look nice. The owner, Chris, is very friendly and accommodating. The instructors are wonderful- whether you're a newbie or seasoned spinner, they'll encourage you and push you towards your best.

I love that this place has showers!! It saves so much time being able to shower off right there instead of going back home. The sound quality, lights and black lights make the actual workout really fun, more like clubbing than working out.

This is not your typical spin class where you just turn the resistance up and down and go fast and slow. This is a full body workout- you'll be doing crunches, sit-ups, tap backs and all sorts of movements on the bike for a full body workout. You'll do weights to work your arms and you are constantly moving.

Check out Matt's class. He is a ball of energy and I guarantee he'll be dancing at more than one given point during the workout. You'll have so much fun you'll forget that your legs are on fire and your calories are screaming as they burn.

This studio is worth checking out, you won't regret it.< /text>

Freedom Ride is absolutely a beautiful and chic studio. Chris did a great job with the design and details. He goes above and beyond to make sure you're pleased, and warmly welcomes you. My experience with all the staff and different instructors have been positive, and I thank you!

<text>Freedom is absolutely terrific, let me break it down.

The facility first of all is clean, well equipped, and trendy putting you in a great mindset to optimize your ride from the get go. The front desk crew always smiles and remembers your name in a genuine way. The instructors have talent not just a cookie cutter class. This is rhythm riding at its finest because of the talent, they will make the class flow perfection. My biggest frustration in rhythm riding is transitions. A lot of instructors will have pauses between songs causing heart rate reductions and flow interruptions that hinder your gains. Freedom is well known for their legendary soundtracks and smooth transitions that reduce any gaps or performance loss.

This was my first time at a new dentist since moving to San Francisco and I was so happy I chose this one. Before going, I read many reviews and patients were saying how nice the staff was here.. and they were right! Tech is up to date, simple to use, and April is sweet and efficient. Arriving to the practice, the COVID precautions were standard: waiting room only held 3 people, sanitizer before entering, plastic shield to protect the front desk workers, and masks on. Since it was my first time there, April gave me a short tour of the place along with good-to-knows about the rest of the staff, it helped me feel comfortable at a new dentist. < Review>
Walking in from a great comedy show at 10:45 p.m., it takes a second for your eyes to adjust to the dim lighting. The drinks are reasonably priced, and there's space towards the back of the long skinny bar for your group. I ended up sitting facing the door, which means the projected screen playing... Something old?... Was behind me. I probably would have been distracted by it if I'd been facing it.

I had a Paloma and it was pretty good, strong and not too sweet. It fit the crazy conversation we were having on top of it, which is to say it was loud but not too loud to be incredulous at your friend. Not my favorite bar, but definitely not one to avoid, either.<//Review>

< Review>
My experience at The Wok Experience?  Meh.  I've experienced better.

Pros-
Inexpensive prices
Lots of food
Clean environment

Cons-
The food

Whenever I'd head to Ellen's Pinoy Grille for some sisig, I would oftentimes browse around The Wok Experience.  I'd see 20% off for seniors, lunch specials etc. displayed on the windows.  I'm a Panda Express regular, so if I would compare the two, my judgement would be-

The Wok Experience is more a Hong Kong Express than a Panda Express

The food items, while plentiful & more varied than Panda Express, look to have been sitting around for a long time.  Also, nothing looked enticing, like "Ooo, yeah I'll have that!".  Soggy orange chicken, sad looking fried rice, BBQ pork that's tough & generally not appetizing.

Service was okay.  The Wok Experience does have plenty of seating going for it.  Available parking around the shopping center.  Plus, with the aforementioned specials, people don't have to pay much for a meal.  However, Chinese fast food restaurants are a dime a dozen, and the lesser quality ones just don't cut it for me.

When I'm back here shopping at the adjacent Walgreens and looking for something to eat,   methinks I'll stick to my tried and true, Ellen's Pinoy Grille, than go back to the Wok Experience.  Unappealing & not quality-focused fresh food, Panda Express will continue to have my business.  At least they give fortune cookies.</Review>

PROS: 1.) NICE DRIVER: The person who picked me up was a really nice guy. We had a great conversation. 2.) NOT CROWDED: They weren't too busy or crowded when I went to get the car. 3.) CLEAN CAR: The car was really clean. 4.) TEXT REMINDERS: I got a nice text reminder about returning my car.

I whispered so as to not cause any scene or embarrassment. Besides, which is more likely: that I, who had only one purpose while I was waiting - to hear my name and respond - would miss my own name, or that in the crush of business the counter people, being human, would make a mistake and overlook me?
3. If all I need is paperwork, offer to email it to me and let me go. Can't be that hard to do.

Otherwise, it all went well. Pricing was good, hours were observed, checking in to rent was quick enough. It's a convenient enough location, but there is a real dearth of parking, and the street is too busy, generally, to allow a left turn from the rental lot.<//text>< pics>

I was hoping for great things here, but it was just mediocre at best for me.  It looks like it has great potential, but this time around the course was in pretty rough shape.  Tee boxes were being re-seeded so boxes were all over the place causing really long or really short holes.  Multiple holes were cart path only which really slowed everything down. Fairways were really tight and patchy, and rough was hit or miss.  Greens rolled true, but very difficult to read as once your in the mountains it rolls downhill even though putt looks uphill.  A few beautiful scenic holes, but the rest of the layout was just meh.  Imo Glen Ivy is much better layed out and in better shape.  Perhaps in good course shape, it would be a better experience, but course right now is a bit beat up.< /review>

< text>
For such a touted course this is one of the worse course that I have ever played on.  My local executive 18 hole golf course David L. Baker has more grass and is in better shape than this course.  I have been to this course three times now and every time I try and give this course a chance it seems to show why I think the course is garbage.  First time I was there there was on a December Saturday and there was no marshal or starter on course at all so there was a train of golf carts waiting to tee off the first hole.  It took me a good 35 minutes from my tee time before I could even put a tee on the ground.  By the time I was almost ready to tee off a guy in front of my group decided to bring his 5 year old son and 3 year old daughter to the course so that daddy can play golf and don't have to pay a baby sitter.  While waiting and waiting the teenager that was in our group got feed up and decided to tee off.  It apparently almost hit the little boy so the dad drove back and confronted the teenager and they almost got into a fist fight.  Again no marshal or starter anywhere in sight to regulate pace of play or to tell the stupid dad that his 5 year old son should not be teeing off from the white tees.  So I decided to leave and go play Glen Ivy instead.  Lost two hours of my time.  I have now come back to the course two different times and the course condition has gotten worse and worse.  You can tell right away that the only aspect of the course that the ground crews actually takes care of are the greens.  The fairways are a joke.  If you have not hitting off dirt than you are hitting off green painted dirt.  I could not believe that a course that is suppose to be on the higher end of the spectrum would actually paint their fairways green to try and make it look as though there is grass.  What grass there is, it is yellow at best.  So if you like hitting off green painted fairways, don't mind 6 hour rounds, but want really nice greens then come here.  But I am done with this place for good unless other people shows me proof otherwise.  My recommendation to everyone is save your time and money and go to Hidden Valley or Glen Ivy.  At least there is real grass to hit off of.</text>
